(B[m#!/bin/bash
echo "is it morning? please answer yes or no"
read timeofday
case "$timeofday" in
	yes | y | YES | Yes) echo "good morning";;
	n* | N* ) echo "good afternoon";;
	y) echo "good monring";;
	*) echo "ans not recognized";;
esac

(B[m#!/bin/bash
showarg()
{
	a=1
	for i in $*
		do
			echo "the $a no arg is $i"
			a=`expr $a + 1`
		done
}
echo "listing start"
showarg $*
echo "total: $#"
echo "listing end"
